---
title: "HP Laser printer wireless: two devices for the same printer"
date: 2017-06-11
forum: Hardware
---

### Post by luca-dgh on 2017-06-11
I recently bought a HP LJ 1102w wireless printer, I configured it for my home network and installed with Hplip 3.17.4.
Now in the printer manager I have a device for my printer and another generic davice called "laserjet". I tried to delete it, but it is immediately re-created.
In the print window the same device is called "HP1102W.local".

Does anybody knows why I have those 2 devices? Is it possible to delete it?

### Post by ajgreeny on 2017-06-11
In a web-browser go to [http://localhost:631/](http://localhost:631/) and in the Administration tab go to Manage Printers.

You may find the generic "laserjet" there, as cups will often add printers it detects automatically.  When you subsequently add that same printer using hplip-toolbox (is that how you did it?) it can show as a duplicate in your Printing dialogue.

---

### Post by efflandt on 2017-06-11
Ubuntu sometimes finds network printers automatically using avahi-daemon and avahi-dnsconfd, which looks for other computers and devices based on Apple ZeroConfig, so the name that shows up is usually the name set in the printer itself for Apple ZeroConfig settings. In my case that would sometimes replicate my Lexmark network printers with the same name, so I set a description of "home" (or "office" for similar printers at work for laptop/tablet I might take to work) for the ones I configured myself in Ubuntu, to be able to chose the specific one I was looking for when printing. But I have not used an HP printer since my old HP LJ 4L (parallel connected to print server) was retired when it got a permanent paper jam I could not find.

---
